TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE 
 
 
 201
THE COMMISSIONER OF LAND ADMINISTRATION, CHEPAUK, CHENNAI 600 005.
Acquisition of Lands
Roc.No.S1/9832/2020
No.VI(1)/325/2020.
 
Notice Under sub-section (1) Of Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001   (Tamil Nadu  Act 34/2002), read with 
Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws  (Revival  Of Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below to be acquired for the 
public purpose, that is for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Perur Chettipalayam Village of Perur 
Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it having already  been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
Lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction and Maintenance), 
Coimbatore and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest in the said Lands as 
the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002.)
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002),  the Governor of Tamil 
Nadu State, hereby acquires that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of 95,480 Square meters 
of Dry Lands. To the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Perur 
Chettipalayam village of Perur Taluk, in Coimbatore District.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Coimbatore District, Perur Taluk, Perur Chettipalayam Village.

Notice Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002), read with Tamil 
Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of  Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019). 
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands  speciﬁ ed in the schedule below to be acquired for the 
public purpose, that is for  the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Nanjundapuram  Village of Coimbatore 
(North) Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it having  already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be 
awarded for  the Lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief  Engineer, Highways (Construction and 
Maintenance), Coimbatore and after  having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having  interest in 
the said Lands as the case may be, do hereby publish the following  notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways  Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition  Laws (Revival Of Operation, 
Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu  Act 38/2019). 
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001  (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Commissioner 
of Land Administration (FAC),  hereby acquires that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to  an extent of 
3252 Square meters of Dry Lands, to the same, a little more or less  is needed for the construction of Western Ring-road to 
Coimbatore City,  between KM 166/6 of Salem - Cochin Road and KM 360/6 of NH 67  Nagapattinam - Gudalur - Mysore Road, 
in Nanjundapuram Village of  Coimbatore (North) Taluk, in Coimbatore District. 
The plan of the Lands under acquisition is kept at the oﬃ  ce of the District  Collector, Coimbatore and in the oﬃ  ce of the Special 
Tahsildar (LA) Unit - I, Western  Ring Road and Mettupalayam Bypass Roads at Taluk oﬃ  ce, Madukkarai may be  inspected at 
any time during oﬃ  ce hours.

Nadu Land Acquisition Laws  (Revival  Of Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
 
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below to be acquired for 
the public purpose, that is for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Theethipalayam Village of Perur 
Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it having already  been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
Lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction and Maintenance), 
Coimbatore and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest in the said Lands as 
the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment And 
Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).

of Land Administration (FAC), hereby acquires that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of 
1,44,830 Square meters of Dry Lands, to the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring-road to 
Coimbatore City Theethipalayam Village of Perur Taluk, in Coimbatore District.

 239
(Roc.No.S1/9840/2020.)
No.VI(1)/329/2020.
Notice Under Sub-Section(1) Of  Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002) and Tamil Nadu 
Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment And Validation ) Act 2019, (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be acquired  for 
the public purpose, that is, for the construction of Western Ring – road to Coimbatore City, in Sundakkamuthur Village of Perur 
Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it has already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
Lands, is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction and Maintenance), 
Chennai and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest on the said Lands, as 
the case may be, de hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 
(Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002).
NOTICE 
 
Under sub- section (1) of section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002), the Commissioner of 
Land Acquisition , hereby acquires that the lads speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of 49,530 square 
meters of Dry Lands, To the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring – road to Coimbatore City, 
between Km 166/6 of Salem – Kochin Road and Km 360/6 of NH 67 Nagapattinam – Gudalur – Mysore Raod, in Sundakkamuthur 
Village of Perur Taluk, in Coimbatore District.
The plan of Lands under acquisition is kept at the oﬃ  ce of the District Collector, Coimbatore and in the Oﬃ  ce of the Spl.
Tahsildar (LA) Western Ring Road at Madukkarai Taluk Oﬃ  ce may be inspected at anytime during oﬃ  ce hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Coimbatore District, Perur Taluk, Sundakkamuthur Village.

the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws(Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019.
         The Governor of Tamil Nadu  having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are required for the 
Highways purpose to wit for construction of Road Over Bridge in lieu of Level Crossing No.20 at Km. 52/4 of Nagai – Gudalore 
- Mysore road in between Railway Km 27/700-900 at Needamangalam Railway Station Yard of Thanjavur – Nagore - Karaikal 
Section and it has already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for Land is to be paid by Divisional 
Engineer Highways (Projects), Thanjavur and after considering  the cause shown by owner or other person having interest on such 
Lands as the case may be do here by publish the following notice under sub section (1) of section 15 of the Highways Act,2001 
(TN Act 34/2002) read with the Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws(Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019.
NOTICE

Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws(Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019. The Government of Tamil Nadu 
here by acquires the Land speciﬁ ed in the schedule below measuring to an extent of 0.02.00  hectares of Lands a little more or 
less required to wit for construction of Road Over Bridge in lieu of Level Crossing No.20 at Km. 52/4 of Nagai – Gudalore - Mysore 
road in between Railway Km 27/700-900 at Needamangalam Railway Station Yard of Thanjavur – Nagore - Karaikal Section in 
Tiruvarur District,

Notice Under sub-section(1) of  Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002) and Tamil Nadu Land 
Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment And Validation ) Act 2019, (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019). 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be acquired  for 
the public purpose, that is, for the construction of Western Ring – road to Coimbatore City, in Narasimmanaiyakkan Palayam 
of North Taluk in Coimbatore District, and it has already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be 
awarded for the Lands, is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction 
and Maintenance), Chennai and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest 
on the said Lands, as the case may be, de hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002).
NOTICE 
Under sub- section (1) of section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002), the Commissioner 
of Land Acquisition , hereby acquires that the lads speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of 34,505 
square meters of Dry Lands, To the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring – road to 
Coimbatore City, Narasimmanaiyakkan Palayam of North Taluk in Coimbatore District.
The plan of Lands under acquisition is kept at the oﬃ  ce of the District Collector, Coimbatore and in the Oﬃ  ce of the 
Spl.Tahsildar (LA) Western Ring Road at Madukkarai Taluk Oﬃ  ce may be inspected at anytime during oﬃ  ce hours.

Roc.No.S1/9837/2020 
 
 
 
                                 
No. VI(1)/332/2020.—
Notice under Sub-Section (1) Of Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu  Act 34/2002), read with 
Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws  (Revival  Of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below to be acquired 
for the public purpose, that is for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Vadavalli Village of Perur 
Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it having already  been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded 
for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction and 
Maintenance), Coimbatore and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest 
in the said lands as the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of 
Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019). 
 
 
    
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002),  the Commissioner 
of Land Administration (FAC), hereby acquires that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent 
of 108888 Square meters of Dry Lands, to the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western 
Ring-road to Coimbatore City Vadavalli Village of Perur Taluk, in Coimbatore District.

Roc.No.S1/9838/2020. 
 
 
 
                                 
No.VI(i)/333/2020.— 
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below to be acquired for 
the public purpose, that is for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Kurudam Palayam village of 
North Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it having already  been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be 
awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction 
and Maintenance), Coimbatore and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having 
interest in the said lands as the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of 
section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws 
(Revival Of Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019). 
 
 
    


Sep. 23, 2020] 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE 
 
 
 265
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002),  the Commissioner 
of Land Administration (FAC), hereby acquires that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of 
77705 Square meters of Dry Lands, to the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring-road 
to Coimbatore City Kurudam Palayam Village of North Taluk, in Coimbatore District.

Notice Under Section 15 (1) of Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tn Act 34 of 2002) Read With Tamil Nadu Act 38 of 2019
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having  been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below have to be acquired under 
Highways purpose to wit for construction of Railway Over Bridge (LC-15) at Thozhur Village, Tiruvallur Taluk, Tiruvallur  District, 
and it had already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands to be paid out of the funds 
controlled and  managed by the Chief Engineer(General), Highways Department and after having considered the cause shown 
by the owner or other persons having interest in the said lands, as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under 
Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (TN Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby notiﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below measuring to extent of 378 Sq. mtr., Dry land in 
S.No.490/1A1F and etc., at  Thozhur  Village, Tiruvallur Taluk, Tiruvallur District, to be the same, a little more or less needed 
for construction of Railway Over Bridge (LC-15). 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the oﬃ  ce of the District Revenue Oﬃ  cer, Tiruvallur,  may be inspected at 
any time during the oﬃ  ce hours.

Notice Under sub-section (1) Of Section 15 Of Tamilnadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamilnadu Act 34/2002), read with Tamil 
Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
 
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be acquired 
for the public purpose, that is for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Somayampalayam village 
of North Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it having already  been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be 
awarded for the Lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction and 
Maintenance), Coimbatore and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest in 
the said Lands as the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, 
Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002),  the Commissioner of 
Land Administration (FAC) hereby acquire the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of 85,390 Square 
meters of Dry Lands. To the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City 
Somayampalayam village of North Taluk, in Coimbatore District.
The plan of the Lands under acquisition is kept at the oﬃ  ce of the District Collector, Coimbatore and n the oﬃ  ce of the Special 
Tahsildar (LA), Western Ring Road Project at Taluk Oﬃ  ce, Madukkarai may be inspected at anytime during oﬃ  ce hours.
Coimbatore (North) Taluk, Somayampalayam Village.

85390
(Roc.No.S1/11340/2020)
No.VI(1)/339/2020.
Notice Under Sub-Section (1) Of Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002), read with Tamil 
Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below have to be acquired for 
the public purpose, that is for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Pannimadai Village of North Taluk, 
in Coimbatore District, and it having already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the Lands is 
to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction and Maintenance), Coimbatore 
and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest in the said Lands as the case 
may do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 
(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 
2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).  
  
N඗ගඑඋඍ
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Commissioner 
of Land Administration (FAC), hereby acquires that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of 
1,47,175 Square meters of Dry Lands, to the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring-road to 
Coimbatore City Pannimadai Village of North Taluk, in Coimbatore District.
The plan of the Lands under acquisition is kept at the oﬃ  ce of the District Collector, Coimbatore and in the oﬃ  ce of the Special 
Tahsildar (LA), Western Ring Road Project at Taluk oﬃ  ce, Madukkarai may be inspected at anytime during oﬃ  ce hours.

(Roc.No.S1/11341/20)
No.VI(1)/340/2020.
Notice Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act, 34/2002), read with Tamil 
Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below have to be acquired 
for the public purpose, that is for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore City in Gudalur South  Village of North 
Taluk, in Coimbatore District, and it having already  been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
Lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (Construction and Maintenance), 
Coimbatore and after having considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest in the said Lands as 
the case may be, do hereby publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and 
Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).


Sep. 23, 2020] 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE 
 
 
 303
N඗ගඑඋඍ
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002),  the Commissioner of 
Land Administration (FAC), hereby acquires the Lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring to an extent of  80448 
Square meters of Dry Lands. To the same, a little more or less is needed for the construction of Western Ring-road to Coimbatore 
City Gudalur South  Village of North Taluk, in Coimbatore District.
The plan of the Lands under acquisition is kept at the oﬃ  ce of the District Collector, Coimbatore and  the oﬃ  ce of the Special 
Tahsildar (LA) Unit-I, Western Ring Road Project at Taluk Oﬃ  ce, Madukkari may be inspected at anytime during oﬃ  ce hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Coimbatore District, Coimbatore North Taluk, Gudalur (South) Village.

Sep. 23, 2020] 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE 
 
 
 315
(Roc.No.S1/9836/20)
No.VI(1)/341/2020.
Notice Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 Of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002), read with Tamil 
Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival Of Operation, Amendment And Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu Act 38/2019).
 The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁ ed that the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below are to be acquired 
for the purpose of construction of the Mettupalayam bye pass in the Village of Chikadasampalayam  Municipality in the Taluk of 
Mettupalayam  in the district of Coimbatore is required for Highways and public purposes, hereby acquire the lands speciﬁ ed in 
the schedule below and measuring  143624.5 Sq. meters and as  already decided, the amount of compensation to be awarded 
for the lands is to be paid out of funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer, Highways (C&M), Chennai and after having 
considered the cause shown by the owners or the other persons having interest in the said lands as the case may, do hereby 
publish the following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 
34 of 2002) read with Tamil Nadu Land Acquisition Laws (Revival of Operation, Amendment and Validation) Act, 2019 (Tamil Nadu 
Act 38/2019). 
 
 
 
             
 N඗ගඑඋඍ
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 ( Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002 ) the Commissioner of 
Land Administration (FAC), hereby acquires the lands speciﬁ ed in the schedule below and measuring  143624.5 S.q meters to the 
same, a little more or less are needed for the purpose for the Mettupalayam Bye pass.   
The Sketches for the above and land acquisition ﬁ elds can be viewed during the oﬃ  ce hours in the oﬃ  ce of Sub-collector, 
Coimbatore North.  
The plan of the lands under acquisition is kept at the oﬃ  ce of the District Collector, Coimbatore and in the oﬃ  ce of the Special 
Tahsildar (LA), Mettupalayam Bye pass – Mettupalayam at Taluk oﬃ  ce, may be inspected at anytime during oﬃ  ce hours.
Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Coimbatore District, Mettupalayam Taluk, Chikkadhasampalayam Village.
